    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<div id="review_3609346351" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3609346351" />
    <a title="Grady" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1362506-grady"><img alt="Grady" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442472304p2/1362506.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3609346351?book_show_action=true">Oct 23, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Grady" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Grady" href="/user/show/1362506-grady">Grady</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3609346351" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7849291431843109607">Dreams and their significances…<br/><br/>Minnesota author Timothy Dorr writes short stories and poems and appears to have both a novel and a poetry anthology due out in 2021. A CONNECTION TO JOHN LENNON? is a short story that suggests that a quality writer will soon be recognized!<br/><br/>Relating this fascinating little story through the character of his daughter Emily makes this traversal of the last mid century even more accessible. Emily approaches her father for a paranormal story for her English class assign</span>
  <span id="freeText7849291431843109607" style="display:none">Dreams and their significances…<br /><br />Minnesota author Timothy Dorr writes short stories and poems and appears to have both a novel and a poetry anthology due out in 2021. A CONNECTION TO JOHN LENNON? is a short story that suggests that a quality writer will soon be recognized!<br /><br />Relating this fascinating little story through the character of his daughter Emily makes this traversal of the last mid century even more accessible. Emily approaches her father for a paranormal story for her English class assignment due the next day, and in doing so encourages her father (Tim Door) to relate his mesmerizing dream that occurred the night John Lennon was killed – December 8, 1980. In recalling his dream for his daughter Tim exorcises the events leading up to that memorable day, memories of his sisters and their infatuation with the Beatles, getting an autograph from Muhammad Ali on a dollar bill, meeting a writer – Susan Braudy - who for her story about Sal Mineo’s suspicious death asks Tim to write a song lyric for her book, his walking past the Dakota Apartments (John Lennon’s abode) on that memorable day in December, and his dream of seeing the Beatles minus Lennon before dawn on December 9 revealed the news of Lennon’s murder. Connecton? Yes, and a satisfying tale for Emily’s paranormal story project.<br /><br />Well written and rich in memorabilia, this little story bodes well for a successful career in writing novels for Timothy Door. Short, but very entertaining and a font of reminiscence. <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7849291431843109607" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer3613643377" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5444460645972239776">A Connection to Lennon? is a short story about the authors unusual dream on the night John Lennon was killed. It's written from the prospective of the authors high school aged daughter and this is done very well. The dream itself is spooky and definitely a strange occurrence. A really nice quick read.</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_3551252436" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3551252436" />
    <a title="Anthony" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/118011158-anthony"><img alt="Anthony" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3551252436?book_show_action=true">Sep 16, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anthony" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anthony" href="/user/show/118011158-anthony">Anthony</a>
      </span>

          added it




        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3551252436" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16787937707828563203">This tells the story of a young daughter writing a paper for class. She asks her Dad for help and so he tells her the story of his dream on the night of John Lennon's death. The story takes you through a web of smaller stories, which were interesting and held my attention. Any fan of the Beatles and that era should give this one a read. It's not only a cool story but also a way to reconnect with that period. Give it a shot!</span>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('32AvA9ehs+848jUzqNnqbEliXjKWIdQ96qmWsN1Pvr6De967aO8chEgIADI7JbNc4MbJkHJkHkh+Rb4YRSYKGA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('GqzGqxY8YTHT2iwvMtaKFUtFGDea08xRNkPCahxiESdGtzcTqXLOWqMgGS6hKtMl4uGPlX6WBiSir+rChAulgQ==')})
  }
